    81	func (t *Turbostat) Init() error {
    82	        if t.Path == "" {
    83	                t.Path = "turbostat"
    84	        }
    85	
    86	        if t.Interval <= 0 {
    87	                t.Interval = config.Duration(10 * time.Second)
    88	        }
    89	
    90	        // Build the command line to spawn Turbostat.
    91	        t.command = make([]string, 0, 10)
    92	        if t.UseSudo {
    93	                t.command = append(t.command, "sudo")
    94	        }
    95	        interval := strconv.FormatFloat(time.Duration(t.Interval).Seconds(), 'f', -1, 64)
    96	        t.command = append(t.command, t.Path, "--quiet", "--interval", interval, "--show", "all")
    97	
    98	        return nil
    99	}
   100	
   101	func (t *Turbostat) Start(acc telegraf.Accumulator) error {
   102	        var err error
   103	        t.process, err = process.New(t.command, nil)
   104	        if err != nil {
   105	                return fmt.Errorf("failed to create process %s: %w", t.command, err)
   106	        }
   107	
   108	        // Read error lines from Turbostat stderr and add them to the accumulator.
   109	        t.process.ReadStderrFn = func(r io.Reader) {
   110	                scanner := bufio.NewScanner(r)
   111	                for scanner.Scan() {
   112	                        acc.AddError(errors.New(scanner.Text()))
   113	                }
   114	                acc.AddError(scanner.Err())
   115	        }
   116	
   117	        // Read metrics from Turbostat stdout and add them to the accumulator.
   118	        // Add any error to the accumulator and continue processing the next lines.
   119	        t.process.ReadStdoutFn = func(r io.Reader) {
   120	                scanner := bufio.NewScanner(r)
   121	                if !scanner.Scan() {
   122	                        acc.AddError(scanner.Err())
   123	                        return
   124	                }
   125	                header := scanner.Text()
   126	                columns := make([]column, 0, 50)
   127	                for _, s := range strings.Fields(header) {
   128	                        columns = append(columns, createColumn(s))
   129	                }
   130	                for scanner.Scan() {
   131	                        line := scanner.Text()
   132	                        if line == header {
   133	                                continue
   134	                        }
   135	                        values := strings.Fields(line)
   136	                        acc.AddError(processValues(acc, columns, values))
   137	                }
   138	                acc.AddError(scanner.Err())
   139	        }
   140	
   141	        t.process.StopOnError = false
   142	        t.process.Log = t.Log
   143	
   144	        if err = t.process.Start(); err != nil {
   145	                return fmt.Errorf("failed to start process %s: %w", t.command, err)
   146	        }
   147	        return nil
   148	}
   149	
   150	func (t *Turbostat) Stop() {
   151	        t.process.Stop()
   152	}
   153	
   154	func (*Turbostat) Gather(telegraf.Accumulator) error {
   155	        return nil
   156	}
   157	
   158	// Creates a metric from columns and values, and adds it to an accumulator.
   159	func processValues(acc telegraf.Accumulator, columns []column, values []string) error {
   160	        if len(values) > len(columns) {
   161	                return fmt.Errorf("too many values: %d columns, %d values", len(columns), len(values))
   162	        }
   163	        tags := make(map[string]string, len(values))
   164	        fields := make(map[string]any, len(values))
   165	        timestamp := time.Now()
   166	        for i, value := range values {
   167	                column := columns[i]
   168	                switch {
   169	                case column.isTime:
   170	                        f, err := strconv.ParseFloat(value, 64)
   171	                        if err != nil {
   172	                                return fmt.Errorf("unable to parse time: %w", err)
   173	                        }
   174	                        timestamp = time.Unix(0, int64(f*1e9))
   175	                case column.isTag:
   176	                        tags[column.name] = value
   177	                default:
   178	                        v, err := strconv.ParseFloat(value, 64)
   179	                        if err != nil {
   180	                                return fmt.Errorf("unable to parse column %q: %w", column.name, err)
   181	                        }
   182	                        fields[column.name] = v
   183	                }
   184	        }
   185	        if len(fields) == 0 {
   186	                return errors.New("no value for any field")
   187	        }
   188	        acc.AddFields("turbostat", fields, tags, timestamp)
   189	        return nil
   190	}
   191	
   192	// Creates a column struct from a Turbostat column name.
   193	func createColumn(s string) column {
   194	        // Add underscores around words known not to have delimiters.
   195	        s = replacer.Replace(s)
   196	        // Split the column name into lower case tokens.
   197	        tokens := splitter.FindAllString(strings.ToLower(s), -1)
   198	        // Expand abbreviations into full words.
   199	        for i, token := range tokens {
   200	                if replacement, found := abbreviations[token]; found {
   201	                        tokens[i] = replacement
   202	                }
   203	        }
   204	
   205	        // Create and return the column.
   206	        name := strings.Join(tokens, "_")
   207	        switch name {
   208	        case "time_of_day_seconds":
   209	                return column{name: name, isTime: true}
   210	        case "package", "node", "die", "core", "cpu", "apic", "x2apic":
   211	                return column{name: name, isTag: true}
   212	        default:
   213	                return column{name: name}
   214	        }
   215	}
   216

   218	        inputs.Add("turbostat", func() telegraf.Input {
   219	                return &Turbostat{}
   220	        })
   221	}

    74	        }
    75	        for _, tt := range tests {
    76	                t.Run(fmt.Sprintf("%s", tt.values), func(t *testing.T) {
    77	                        acc := &testutil.Accumulator{}
    78	                        err := processValues(acc, columns, tt.values)
    79	                        require.NoError(t, err)
    80	                        actual := acc.GetTelegrafMetrics()
    81	                        testutil.RequireMetricsEqual(t, []telegraf.Metric{tt.metric}, actual, testutil.IgnoreTime())
    82	                })
    83	        }
    84	}
    85	
    86	func TestProcessValuesErrors(t *testing.T) {
    87	        columns := []column{
    88	                {name: "cpu", isTag: true},
    89	                {name: "core", isTag: true},
    90	                {name: "busy_frequency_mhz", isTag: false},
    91	                {name: "core_power_watt", isTag: false},
    92	        }
    93	        tests := []struct {
    94	                values []string
    95	                err    string
    96	        }{
    97	                {
    98	                        values: []string{"0", "1"},
    99	                        err:    "no value for any field",
   100	                },
   101	                {
   102	                        values: []string{"0", "1", "123", "456", "789"},
   103	                        err:    "too many values: 4 columns, 5 values",
   104	                },
   105	                {
   106	                        values: []string{"0", "1", "xyz"},
   107	                        err:    "unable to parse column \"busy_frequency_mhz\": strconv.ParseFloat: parsing \"xyz\": invalid syntax",
   108	                },
   109	        }
   110	        for _, tt := range tests {
   111	                t.Run(fmt.Sprintf("%s", tt.values), func(t *testing.T) {
   112	                        var acc testutil.Accumulator
   113	                        err := processValues(&acc, columns, tt.values)
   114	                        require.ErrorContains(t, err, tt.err)
   115	                })
   116	        }
   117	}
   118	
   119	func TestCases(t *testing.T) {
   120	        dirs, err := os.ReadDir("testcases")
   121	        require.NoError(t, err)
   122	        for _, f := range dirs {
   123	                // Only handle directories.
   124	                if !f.IsDir() {
   125	                        continue
   126	                }
   127	
   128	                testcasePath := filepath.Join("testcases", f.Name())
   129	                configFilename := filepath.Join(testcasePath, "telegraf.conf")
   130	                inputFilename := filepath.Join(testcasePath, "input.txt")
   131	                expectedFilename := filepath.Join(testcasePath, "expected.out")
   132	
   133	                t.Run(f.Name(), func(t *testing.T) {
   134	                        // Load the expected output.
   135	                        parser := &influx.Parser{}
   136	                        require.NoError(t, parser.Init())
   137	                        expected, err := testutil.ParseMetricsFromFile(expectedFilename, parser)
   138	                        require.NoError(t, err)
   139	
   140	                        // Configure the plugin.
   141	                        cfg := config.NewConfig()
   142	                        require.NoError(t, cfg.LoadConfig(configFilename))
   143	                        require.Len(t, cfg.Inputs, 1)
   144	                        plugin := cfg.Inputs[0].Input.(*Turbostat)
   145	                        require.NoError(t, plugin.Init())
   146	
   147	                        // Replace Turbostat with a mock process which outputs the desired lines.
   148	                        exe, err := os.Executable()
   149	                        require.NoError(t, err)
   150	                        plugin.command = []string{exe, "-mockInput=" + inputFilename}
   151	
   152	                        // Start the plugin and wait for the expected metrics.
   153	                        var acc testutil.Accumulator
   154	                        require.NoError(t, plugin.Start(&acc))
   155	
   156	                        require.Eventually(t, func() bool {
   157	                                return acc.NMetrics() == uint64(len(expected))
   158	                        }, 3*time.Second, 100*time.Millisecond)
   159	
   160	                        require.Empty(t, acc.Errors)
   161	
   162	                        actual := acc.GetTelegrafMetrics()
   163	                        testutil.RequireMetricsEqual(t, expected, actual, testutil.IgnoreTime())
   164	                })
   165	        }
   166	}
   167	
   168	// This function lets the test executable to behave as a mock Turbostat process.
   169	func TestMain(m *testing.M) {
   170	        var mockInput string
   171	        flag.StringVar(&mockInput, "mockInput", "", "mock turbostat output")
   172	        flag.Parse()
   173	
   174	        if mockInput == "" {
   175	                os.Exit(m.Run())
   176	        }
   177	
   178	        err := func() error {
   179	                file, err := os.Open(mockInput)
   180	                if err != nil {
   181	                        return err
   182	                }
   183	                defer file.Close()
   184	
   185	                _, err = io.Copy(os.Stdout, file)
   186	                if err != nil {
   187	                        return err
   188	                }
   189	                return nil
   190	        }()
   191	        if err != nil {
   192	                os.Exit(5) // EIO
   193	        }
   194	
   195	        // Sleep. Terminating immediately would look like Turbostat crashed.
   196	        time.Sleep(3 * time.Second)
   197	}
   198

Good, that confirms the issue can be caused by trailing whitespace. But there could be other causes too. Let me think about what other scenarios could cause this:

1. **Trailing whitespace**: header lines may differ in trailing whitespace
2. **Different column order/names**: different samples may have different headers (unlikely but possible)
3. **Blank lines or other non-data lines**: turbostat may output blank lines or other metadata
4. **The header itself may contain "usec" as both a column name AND a value in some context**

Actually, now I realize there might be an even simpler issue. Let me look at the code flow again:

```go
t.process.ReadStdoutFn = func(r io.Reader) {
    scanner := bufio.NewScanner(r)
    if !scanner.Scan() {
        acc.AddError(scanner.Err())
        return
    }
    header := scanner.Text()
    columns := make([]column, 0, 50)
    for _, s := range strings.Fields(header) {
        columns = append(columns, createColumn(s))
    }
    for scanner.Scan() {
        line := scanner.Text()
        if line == header {
            continue
        }
        values := strings.Fields(line)
        acc.AddError(processValues(acc, columns, values))
    }
    acc.AddError(scanner.Err())
}
```

What if `header` is empty (first line is blank)? Then `strings.Fields(header)` returns an empty slice, `columns` is empty, and every subsequent line would be compared to an empty string. If no line is empty, no line matches, so all lines would be processed as data. But with an empty columns list, `processValues` would fail with "too many values" error.

But wait, what if the first line is something like a summary line that has different columns? Like:
```
turbostat version 2024.07.26 - ...
```

Then columns would be created from that, and the real header would be processed as data. But the error would be about parsing "usec" for the "turbostat" column, not for the "usec" column.

Unless... the first line has columns that include "usec" somehow? That seems unlikely.

Let me think about this differently. The error is:
```
unable to parse column "usec": strconv.ParseFloat: parsing "usec": invalid syntax
```

The column name is "usec", which means the header was parsed correctly and "usec" is one of the columns. The value is "usec", which means a line being processed as data has "usec" as a value for that column.

This can only happen if:
1. A duplicate header line is processed as data (the duplicate header check fails)
2. Some other line with "usec" as a value is output by turbostat

For case 1, the fix would be to make the duplicate header detection more robust.

For case 2, the fix would be to skip lines that can't be parsed.

Let me look at whether there's a better approach. Instead of comparing raw lines, we could compare the parsed fields. If a line's fields, when parsed, look like they match the column names (i.e., they're a header), skip it.

But actually, I think the simplest and most robust fix is:

1. Trim spaces from both `header` and `line` before comparing
2. Also check if any value in a data line matches the corresponding column name (which would indicate it's a header line)

But wait, there's another approach: we could simply skip lines where a field value equals the corresponding column name. For example, if we have a column named "usec" and the value is "usec", that's likely a repeated header.

Actually, the simplest approach is to trim spaces before comparing. But there could be other whitespace differences too (like tabs vs spaces). Let me think of a more robust solution.

Looking at the test data, the header line has fields separated by tabs/spaces. A more robust approach would be to check if the fields of a line match the column names (i.e., if `values[i] == columns[i].name` for all i, or if the set of values matches the set of column names).

But actually, looking at the AMD test data, some column values could match their names coincidentally. For example, a column named "C1" could have a value "C1". But that's unlikely.

I think the best fix is to use `strings.TrimSpace` on both the header and the line before comparing. But also, to be even more robust, we should check if the line, when split into fields, matches the column names. If all values in a line match the corresponding column names, it's definitely a header.

Let me implement the fix

func createColumn(s string) column {
        // Add underscores around words known not to have delimiters.
        s = replacer.Replace(s)
        // Split the column name into lower case tokens.
        tokens := splitter.FindAllString(strings.ToLower(s), -1)
        // Expand abbreviations into full words.
        for i, token := range tokens {
                if replacement, found := abbreviations[token]; found {
                        tokens[i] = replacement
                }
        }

        // Create and return the column.
        name := strings.Join(tokens, "_")
        switch name {
        case "time_of_day_seconds":
                return column{name: name, isTime: true}
        case "package", "node", "die", "core", "cpu", "apic", "x2apic":
                return column{name: name, isTag: true}
        default:
                return column{name: name}
        }
}

// Checks if a line of values matches the column names, indicating it is a header line.
func isHeaderLine(columns []column, values []string) bool {
        if len(values) == 0 || len(values) > len(columns) {
                return false
        }
        for i, v := range values {
                if v != columns[i].name {
                        // For the check we use the raw turbostat column name, which
                        // is different from the transformed column name. We need to
                        // check if the value matches the original column header.
                        return false
                }
        }
        return true

    81	func (t *Turbostat) Init() error {
    82	        if t.Path == "" {
    83	                t.Path = "turbostat"
    84	        }
    85	
    86	        if t.Interval <= 0 {
    87	                t.Interval = config.Duration(10 * time.Second)
    88	        }
    89	
    90	        // Build the command line to spawn Turbostat.
    91	        t.command = make([]string, 0, 10)
    92	        if t.UseSudo {
    93	                t.command = append(t.command, "sudo")
    94	        }
    95	        interval := strconv.FormatFloat(time.Duration(t.Interval).Seconds(), 'f', -1, 64)
    96	        t.command = append(t.command, t.Path, "--quiet", "--interval", interval, "--show", "all")
    97	
    98	        return nil
    99	}
   100	
   101	func (t *Turbostat) Start(acc telegraf.Accumulator) error {
   102	        var err error
   103	        t.process, err = process.New(t.command, nil)
   104	        if err != nil {
   105	                return fmt.Errorf("failed to create process %s: %w", t.command, err)
   106	        }
   107	
   108	        // Read error lines from Turbostat stderr and add them to the accumulator.
   109	        t.process.ReadStderrFn = func(r io.Reader) {
   110	                scanner := bufio.NewScanner(r)
   111	                for scanner.Scan() {
   112	                        acc.AddError(errors.New(scanner.Text()))
   113	                }
   114	                acc.AddError(scanner.Err())
   115	        }
   116	
   117	        // Read metrics from Turbostat stdout and add them to the accumulator.
   118	        // Add any error to the accumulator and continue processing the next lines.
   119	        t.process.ReadStdoutFn = func(r io.Reader) {
   120	                scanner := bufio.NewScanner(r)
   121	                if !scanner.Scan() {
   122	                        acc.AddError(scanner.Err())
   123	                        return
   124	                }
   125	                header := scanner.Text()
   126	                headerFields := strings.Fields(header)
   127	                columns := make([]column, 0, 50)
   128	                for _, s := range headerFields {
   129	                        columns = append(columns, createColumn(s))
   130	                }
   131	                for scanner.Scan() {
   132	                        line := scanner.Text()
   133	                        if strings.TrimSpace(line) == strings.TrimSpace(header) {
   134	                                continue
   135	                        }
   136	                        values := strings.Fields(line)
   137	                        if isHeaderLine(headerFields, values) {
   138	                                continue
   139	                        }
   140	                        acc.AddError(processValues(acc, columns, values))
   141	                }
   142	                acc.AddError(scanner.Err())
   143	        }
   144	
   145	        t.process.StopOnError = false
   146	        t.process.Log = t.Log
   147	
   148	        if err = t.process.Start(); err != nil {
   149	                return fmt.Errorf("failed to start process %s: %w", t.command, err)
   150	        }
   151	        return nil
   152	}
   153	
   154	func (t *Turbostat) Stop() {
   155	        t.process.Stop()
   156	}
   157	
   158	func (*Turbostat) Gather(telegraf.Accumulator) error {
   159	        return nil
   160	}
   161	
   162	// Creates a metric from columns and values, and adds it to an accumulator.
   163	func processValues(acc telegraf.Accumulator, columns []column, values []string) error {
   164	        if len(values) > len(columns) {
   165	                return fmt.Errorf("too many values: %d columns, %d values", len(columns), len(values))
   166	        }
   167	        tags := make(map[string]string, len(values))
   168	        fields := make(map[string]any, len(values))
   169	        timestamp := time.Now()
   170	        for i, value := range values {
   171	                column := columns[i]
   172	                switch {
   173	                case column.isTime:
   174	                        f, err := strconv.ParseFloat(value, 64)
   175	                        if err != nil {
   176	                                return fmt.Errorf("unable to parse time: %w", err)
   177	                        }
   178	                        timestamp = time.Unix(0, int64(f*1e9))
   179	                case column.isTag:
   180	                        tags[column.name] = value
   181	                default:
   182	                        v, err := strconv.ParseFloat(value, 64)
   183	                        if err != nil {
   184	                                return fmt.Errorf("unable to parse column %q: %w", column.name, err)
   185	                        }
   186	                        fields[column.name] = v
   187	                }
   188	        }
   189	        if len(fields) == 0 {
   190	                return errors.New("no value for any field")
   191	        }
   192	        acc.AddFields("turbostat", fields, tags, timestamp)
   193	        return nil
   194	}
   195	
   196	// Creates a column struct from a Turbostat column name.
   197	func createColumn(s string) column {
   198	        // Add underscores around words known not to have delimiters.
   199	        s = replacer.Replace(s)
   200	        // Split the column name into lower case tokens.
   201	        tokens := splitter.FindAllString(strings.ToLower(s), -1)
   202	        // Expand abbreviations into full words.
   203	        for i, token := range tokens {
   204	                if replacement, found := abbreviations[token]; found {
   205	                        tokens[i] = replacement
   206	                }
   207	        }
   208	
   209	        // Create and return the column.
   210	        name := strings.Join(tokens, "_")
   211	        switch name {
   212	        case "time_of_day_seconds":
   213	                return column{name: name, isTime: true}
   214	        case "package", "node", "die", "core", "cpu", "apic", "x2apic":
   215	                return column{name: name, isTag: true}
   216	        default:
   217	                return column{name: name}
   218	        }
   219	}
   220	
   221	// Checks if a line of values matches the original header fields, indicating it is a
   222	// repeated header line.
   223	func isHeaderLine(headerFields, values []string) bool {
   224	        if len(values) != len(headerFields) {
   225	                return false
   226	        }
   227	        for i, v := range values {
   228	                if v != headerFields[i] {
   229	                        return false
   230	                }
   231	        }
   232	        return true
   233	}

   236	        inputs.Add("turbostat", func() telegraf.Input {
   237	                return &Turbostat{}
   238	        })
   239	}

+        // Read error lines from Turbostat stderr and add them to the accumulator.
+        t.process.ReadStderrFn = func(r io.Reader) {
+                scanner := bufio.NewScanner(r)
+                for scanner.Scan() {
+                        acc.AddError(errors.New(scanner.Text()))
+                }
+                acc.AddError(scanner.Err())

+        // Add any error to the accumulator and continue processing the next lines.
+        t.process.ReadStdoutFn = func(r io.Reader) {
+                scanner := bufio.NewScanner(r)
+                if !scanner.Scan() {
+                        acc.AddError(scanner.Err())
+                        return
+                }
+                header := scanner.Text()
+                headerFields := strings.Fields(header)
+                columns := make([]column, 0, 50)
+                for _, s := range headerFields {
+                        columns = append(columns, createColumn(s))
+                }
+                for scanner.Scan() {
+                        line := scanner.Text()
+                        if strings.TrimSpace(line) == strings.TrimSpace(header) {
+                                continue
+                        }
+                        values := strings.Fields(line)
+                        if isHeaderLine(headerFields, values) {
+                                continue
+                        }
+                        acc.AddError(processValues(acc, columns, values))
+                }
+                acc.AddError(scanner.Err())
+        }
+
+        t.process.StopOnError = false
+        t.process.Log = t.Log
+
+        if err = t.process.Start(); err != nil {
+                return fmt.Errorf("failed to start process %s: %w", t.command, err)
+        }
+        return nil
 }

 // Creates a metric from columns and values, and adds it to an accumulator.
 func processValues(acc telegraf.Accumulator, columns []column, values []string) error {
-	if len(values) > len(columns) {
-		return fmt.Errorf("too many values: %d columns, %d values", len(columns), len(values))
-	}

-		default:
-			v, err := strconv.ParseFloat(value, 64)
-			if err != nil {
-				return fmt.Errorf("unable to parse column %q: %w", column.name, err)
-			}
-			fields[column.name] = v

+        if len(values) > len(columns) {
+                return fmt.Errorf("too many values: %d columns, %d values", len(columns), len(values))
+        }
+        tags := make(map[string]string, len(values))
+        fields := make(map[string]any, len(values))
+        timestamp := time.Now()
+        for i, value := range values {
+                column := columns[i]
+                switch {
+                case column.isTime:
+                        f, err := strconv.ParseFloat(value, 64)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return fmt.Errorf("unable to parse time: %w", err)
+                        }
+                        timestamp = time.Unix(0, int64(f*1e9))
+                case column.isTag:
+                        tags[column.name] = value
+                default:
+                        v, err := strconv.ParseFloat(value, 64)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return fmt.Errorf("unable to parse column %q: %w", column.name, err)
+                        }
+                        fields[column.name] = v
+                }
+        }
+        if len(fields) == 0 {
+                return errors.New("no value for any field")
+        }
+        acc.AddFields("turbostat", fields, tags, timestamp)
+        return nil
 }
 
 // Creates a column struct from a Turbostat column name.
 func createColumn(s string) column {
-	// Add underscores around words known not to have delimiters.
-	s = replacer.Replace(s)
-	// Split the column name into lower case tokens.
-	tokens := splitter.FindAllString(strings.ToLower(s), -1)
-	// Expand abbreviations into full words.

-		if replacement, found := abbreviations[token]; found {
-			tokens[i] = replacement
-		}
-	}
-

-	switch name {
-	case "time_of_day_seconds":
-		return column{name: name, isTime: true}
-	case "package", "node", "die", "core", "cpu", "apic", "x2apic":
-		return column{name: name, isTag: true}
-	default:
-		return column{name: name}
-	}
+        // Add underscores around words known not to have delimiters.
+        s = replacer.Replace(s)
+        // Split the column name into lower case tokens.
+        tokens := splitter.FindAllString(strings.ToLower(s), -1)
+        // Expand abbreviations into full words.
+        for i, token := range tokens {
+                if replacement, found := abbreviations[token]; found {
+                        tokens[i] = replacement
+                }
+        }
+
+        // Create and return the column.
+        name := strings.Join(tokens, "_")
+        switch name {
+        case "time_of_day_seconds":
+                return column{name: name, isTime: true}
+        case "package", "node", "die", "core", "cpu", "apic", "x2apic":
+                return column{name: name, isTag: true}
+        default:
+                return column{name: name}
+        }
+}
+
+// Checks if a line of values matches the original header fields, indicating it is a
+// repeated header line.
+func isHeaderLine(headerFields, values []string) bool {
+        if len(values) != len(headerFields) {
+                return false
+        }
+        for i, v := range values {
+                if v != headerFields[i] {
+                        return false
+                }
+        }
+        return true
 }

Then every subsequent line fails `isHeaderLine` (len mismatch) and `processValues` returns "too many values" for any non-empty line. But this is an existing issue, not related to my change.

package main

import (
    "fmt"
    "strings"
)

// Simulated column struct
type column struct {
    name   string
    isTag  bool
    isTime bool
}

// Checks if a line of values matches the original header fields, indicating it is a
// repeated header line.
func isHeaderLine(headerFields, values []string) bool {
    if len(values) != len(headerFields) {
        return false
    }
    for i, v := range values {
        if v != headerFields[i] {
            return false
        }
    }
    return true
}

func main() {
    // Simulate the AMD test case header
    header := "usec    Time_Of_Day_Seconds     Core    CPU     APIC    X2APIC  Avg_MHz Busy%   Bzy_MHz TSC_MHz IPC     IRQ     POLL    C1      C2      C3      POLL%   C1%     C2%     C3%     CorWatt PkgWatt"
    
    headerFields := strings.Fields(header)
    fmt.Printf("Header fields: %v\n", headerFields)
    
    // Test 1: Exact match header (should be detected)
    line1 := header
    values1 := strings.Fields(line1)
    fmt.Printf("Test 1 - exact match: %v (expected: true)\n", isHeaderLine(headerFields, values1))
    
    // Test 2: Header with trailing spaces (should be detected by TrimSpace, 
    // but also by isHeaderLine since Fields strips whitespace)
    line2 := header + "  "
    values2 := strings.Fields(line2)
    fmt.Printf("Test 2 - trailing spaces: %v (expected: true)\n", isHeaderLine(headerFields, values2))
    
    // Test 3: Header with different internal spacing (should be detected)
    line3 := "usec Time_Of_Day_Seconds Core CPU APIC X2APIC Avg_MHz Busy% Bzy_MHz TSC_MHz IPC IRQ POLL C1 C2 C3 POLL% C1% C2% C3% CorWatt PkgWatt"
    values3 := strings.Fields(line3)
    fmt.Printf("Test 3 - different spacing: %v (expected: true)\n", isHeaderLine(headerFields, values3))
    
    // Test 4: Actual data line (should NOT be detected as header)
    line4 := "  966   1745932475.967756       -       -       -       -       41      1.20    3431    3793    0.98    30422   1412    2836    10698   15564   0.04    0.33    5.55    93.03   1.12    24.55"
    values4 := strings.Fields(line4)
    fmt.Printf("Test 4 - data line: %v (expected: false)\n", isHeaderLine(headerFields, values4))
    
    // Test 5: TrimSpace comparison
    fmt.Printf("Test 5 - TrimSpace equal: %v (expected: true)\n", strings.TrimSpace(line2) == strings.TrimSpace(header))
    
    fmt.Println("\nAll tests passed!")

}
EOF
go run /tmp/test_fix.go

Let me summarize the changes:\n\n## Summary of Changes\n\nThe issue was that the turbostat plugin was throwing an error: `unable to parse column "usec": strconv.ParseFloat: parsing "usec": invalid syntax`. This happened because:\n\n1. Turbostat outputs the column header line at the beginning and again at each interval\n2. The plugin tries to skip repeated headers by comparing the raw line string: `if line == header { continue }`\n3. If there are any whitespace differences (like trailing spaces), the comparison fails\n4. The header line gets processed as data, and the first value "usec" fails to parse as a float\n\n### Fix:\n1. Added `strings.TrimSpace` to the header comparison to handle trailing whitespace differences\n2. Added a new `isHeaderLine` function that compares the parsed fields of a line against the original header fields. This handles any whitespace differences (tabs vs spaces, multiple spaces, etc.)\n3. Both checks are used to ensure robust detection of repeated header lines\n\nThe fix ensures that repeated header lines are properly detected and skipped, preventing the parse error from occurring.', role='assistant', tool_calls=[ChatCompletionMessageToolCall(index=0, function=Function(arguments='{"command": "submit"}', name='submit'), id='call_9468be9ad3064d5c9e58d3c5', type='function')], function_call=None, provider_specific_fields={'refusal': None}), provider_specific_fields={'content_filter_results': {}})], usage=Usage(completion_tokens=324, prompt_tokens=82122, total_tokens=82446, completion_tokens_details=None, prompt_tokens_details=None, audio_prompt_tokens=0), service_tier=None, prompt_filter_results=None)

+        // Read error lines from Turbostat stderr and add them to the accumulator.
+        t.process.ReadStderrFn = func(r io.Reader) {
+                scanner := bufio.NewScanner(r)
+                for scanner.Scan() {
+                        acc.AddError(errors.New(scanner.Text()))
+                }
+                acc.AddError(scanner.Err())

+        // Add any error to the accumulator and continue processing the next lines.
+        t.process.ReadStdoutFn = func(r io.Reader) {
+                scanner := bufio.NewScanner(r)
+                if !scanner.Scan() {
+                        acc.AddError(scanner.Err())
+                        return
+                }
+                header := scanner.Text()
+                headerFields := strings.Fields(header)
+                columns := make([]column, 0, 50)
+                for _, s := range headerFields {
+                        columns = append(columns, createColumn(s))
+                }
+                for scanner.Scan() {
+                        line := scanner.Text()
+                        if strings.TrimSpace(line) == strings.TrimSpace(header) {
+                                continue
+                        }
+                        values := strings.Fields(line)
+                        if isHeaderLine(headerFields, values) {
+                                continue
+                        }
+                        acc.AddError(processValues(acc, columns, values))
+                }
+                acc.AddError(scanner.Err())
+        }
+
+        t.process.StopOnError = false
+        t.process.Log = t.Log
+
+        if err = t.process.Start(); err != nil {
+                return fmt.Errorf("failed to start process %s: %w", t.command, err)
+        }
+        return nil

+        tags := make(map[string]string, len(values))
+        fields := make(map[string]any, len(values))
+        timestamp := time.Now()
+        for i, value := range values {

+                switch {

+                        f, err := strconv.ParseFloat(value, 64)
+                        if err != nil {

+                        }
+                        timestamp = time.Unix(0, int64(f*1e9))
+                case column.isTag:
+                        tags[column.name] = value
+                default:
+                        v, err := strconv.ParseFloat(value, 64)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return fmt.Errorf("unable to parse column %q: %w", column.name, err)
+                        }
+                        fields[column.name] = v
+                }
+        }
+        if len(fields) == 0 {
+                return errors.New("no value for any field")
+        }
+        acc.AddFields("turbostat", fields, tags, timestamp)
+        return nil

 func createColumn(s string) column {
-	// Add underscores around words known not to have delimiters.

+        // Add underscores around words known not to have delimiters.
+        s = replacer.Replace(s)
+        // Split the column name into lower case tokens.
+        tokens := splitter.FindAllString(strings.ToLower(s), -1)
+        // Expand abbreviations into full words.
+        for i, token := range tokens {
+                if replacement, found := abbreviations[token]; found {
+                        tokens[i] = replacement
+                }
+        }
+
+        // Create and return the column.
+        name := strings.Join(tokens, "_")
+        switch name {
+        case "time_of_day_seconds":
+                return column{name: name, isTime: true}
+        case "package", "node", "die", "core", "cpu", "apic", "x2apic":
+                return column{name: name, isTag: true}
+        default:
+                return column{name: name}
+        }

+
+// Checks if a line of values matches the original header fields, indicating it is a
+// repeated header line.
+func isHeaderLine(headerFields, values []string) bool {
+        if len(values) != len(headerFields) {
+                return false
+        }
+        for i, v := range values {
+                if v != headerFields[i] {
+                        return false
+                }
+        }
+        return true
 }

+        // Read error lines from Turbostat stderr and add them to the accumulator.
+        t.process.ReadStderrFn = func(r io.Reader) {
+                scanner := bufio.NewScanner(r)
+                for scanner.Scan() {
+                        acc.AddError(errors.New(scanner.Text()))
+                }
+                acc.AddError(scanner.Err())
+        }

+        // Read metrics from Turbostat stdout and add them to the accumulator.
+        // Add any error to the accumulator and continue processing the next lines.
+        t.process.ReadStdoutFn = func(r io.Reader) {
+                scanner := bufio.NewScanner(r)
+                if !scanner.Scan() {
+                        acc.AddError(scanner.Err())
+                        return
+                }
+                header := scanner.Text()
+                headerFields := strings.Fields(header)
+                columns := make([]column, 0, 50)
+                for _, s := range headerFields {
+                        columns = append(columns, createColumn(s))
+                }
+                for scanner.Scan() {
+                        line := scanner.Text()
+                        if strings.TrimSpace(line) == strings.TrimSpace(header) {
+                                continue
+                        }
+                        values := strings.Fields(line)
+                        if isHeaderLine(headerFields, values) {
+                                continue
+                        }
+                        acc.AddError(processValues(acc, columns, values))
+                }
+                acc.AddError(scanner.Err())
+        }
+
+        t.process.StopOnError = false
+        t.process.Log = t.Log
+
+        if err = t.process.Start(); err != nil {
+                return fmt.Errorf("failed to start process %s: %w", t.command, err)
+        }
+        return nil
 }

 // Creates a metric from columns and values, and adds it to an accumulator.
 func processValues(acc telegraf.Accumulator, columns []column, values []string) error {
-	if len(values) > len(columns) {
-		return fmt.Errorf("too many values: %d columns, %d values", len(columns), len(values))
-	}
-	tags := make(map[string]string, len(values))

-		default:
-			v, err := strconv.ParseFloat(value, 64)
-			if err != nil {
-				return fmt.Errorf("unable to parse column %q: %w", column.name, err)
-			}
-			fields[column.name] = v

+        if len(values) > len(columns) {
+                return fmt.Errorf("too many values: %d columns, %d values", len(columns), len(values))
+        }
+        tags := make(map[string]string, len(values))
+        fields := make(map[string]any, len(values))
+        timestamp := time.Now()
+        for i, value := range values {
+                column := columns[i]
+                switch {
+                case column.isTime:
+                        f, err := strconv.ParseFloat(value, 64)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return fmt.Errorf("unable to parse time: %w", err)
+                        }
+                        timestamp = time.Unix(0, int64(f*1e9))
+                case column.isTag:
+                        tags[column.name] = value
+                default:
+                        v, err := strconv.ParseFloat(value, 64)
+                        if err != nil {
+                                return fmt.Errorf("unable to parse column %q: %w", column.name, err)
+                        }
+                        fields[column.name] = v
+                }
+        }
+        if len(fields) == 0 {
+                return errors.New("no value for any field")
+        }
+        acc.AddFields("turbostat", fields, tags, timestamp)
+        return nil
 }
 
 // Creates a column struct from a Turbostat column name.
 func createColumn(s string) column {
-	// Add underscores around words known not to have delimiters.
-	s = replacer.Replace(s)
-	// Split the column name into lower case tokens.
-	tokens := splitter.FindAllString(strings.ToLower(s), -1)
-	// Expand abbreviations into full words.
-	for i, token := range tokens {
-		if replacement, found := abbreviations[token]; found {
-			tokens[i] = replacement
-		}
-	}
-
-	// Create and return the column.
-	name := strings.Join(tokens, "_")
-	switch name {
-	case "time_of_day_seconds":
-		return column{name: name, isTime: true}
-	case "package", "node", "die", "core", "cpu", "apic", "x2apic":
-		return column{name: name, isTag: true}
-	default:
-		return column{name: name}
-	}
+        // Add underscores around words known not to have delimiters.
+        s = replacer.Replace(s)
+        // Split the column name into lower case tokens.
+        tokens := splitter.FindAllString(strings.ToLower(s), -1)
+        // Expand abbreviations into full words.
+        for i, token := range tokens {
+                if replacement, found := abbreviations[token]; found {
+                        tokens[i] = replacement
+                }
+        }
+
+        // Create and return the column.
+        name := strings.Join(tokens, "_")
+        switch name {
+        case "time_of_day_seconds":
+                return column{name: name, isTime: true}
+        case "package", "node", "die", "core", "cpu", "apic", "x2apic":
+                return column{name: name, isTag: true}
+        default:
+                return column{name: name}
+        }
+}
+
+// Checks if a line of values matches the original header fields, indicating it is a
+// repeated header line.
+func isHeaderLine(headerFields, values []string) bool {
+        if len(values) != len(headerFields) {
+                return false
+        }
+        for i, v := range values {
+                if v != headerFields[i] {
+                        return false
+                }
+        }
+        return true
 }

-	})
+        inputs.Add("turbostat", func() telegraf.Input {
+                return &Turbostat{}
+        })
 }

+                t.Interval = config.Duration(10 * time.Second)
+        }
+
+        // Build the command line to spawn Turbostat.
+        t.command = make([]string, 0, 10)
+        if t.UseSudo {
+                t.command = append(t.command, "sudo")
+        }
+        interval := strconv.FormatFloat(time.Duration(t.Interval).Seconds(), 'f', -1, 64)
+        t.command = append(t.command, t.Path, "--quiet", "--interval", interval, "--show", "all")
+
+        return nil
 }

+                                continue
+                        }
+                        values := strings.Fields(line)
+                        if isHeaderLine(headerFields, values) {
+                                continue
+                        }
+                        acc.AddError(processValues(acc, columns, values))
+                }
+                acc.AddError(scanner.Err())
+        }
+
+        t.process.StopOnError = false
+        t.process.Log = t.Log
+
+        if err = t.process.Start(); err != nil {
+                return fmt.Errorf("failed to start process %s: %w", t.command, err)
+        }
+        return nil

+                default:

+                }
+        }
+        if len(fields) == 0 {
+                return errors.New("no value for any field")
+        }
+        acc.AddFields("turbostat", fields, tags, timestamp)
+        return nil
 }

+        // Add underscores around words known not to have delimiters.
+        s = replacer.Replace(s)
+        // Split the column name into lower case tokens.
+        tokens := splitter.FindAllString(strings.ToLower(s), -1)
+        // Expand abbreviations into full words.
+        for i, token := range tokens {
+                if replacement, found := abbreviations[token]; found {
+                        tokens[i] = replacement
+                }
+        }
+
+        // Create and return the column.
+        name := strings.Join(tokens, "_")
+        switch name {
+        case "time_of_day_seconds":
+                return column{name: name, isTime: true}
+        case "package", "node", "die", "core", "cpu", "apic", "x2apic":
+                return column{name: name, isTag: true}
+        default:
+                return column{name: name}
+        }
+}
+
+// Checks if a line of values matches the original header fields, indicating it is a
+// repeated header line.
+func isHeaderLine(headerFields, values []string) bool {
+        if len(values) != len(headerFields) {
+                return false
+        }
+        for i, v := range values {
+                if v != headerFields[i] {
+                        return false
+                }
+        }
+        return true
 }
